partName then continue end local part=partName:FindFirstChildOfClass("Model"):Clone()part.Parent=workspace.Blueprints part:SetPrimaryPartCFrame(CFrame)local class=Instance.new("StringValue",part)class.Name="TreeClass"class.Value=treeclass local material=treeclass=="LoneCave"and Enum.Material.Foil or treeclass=="Frost"and Enum.Material.Ice or or Enum.Material.Wood local color=treeclass=="SpookyNeon"and Color3.fromRGB(170,85,0)or treeclass=="Spooky"and Color3.fromRGB(170,85,0)or treeclass=="CaveCrawler"and Color3.fromRGB(16,42,220)or
